'''Race to Rank 15'''<br>
[[File:News-Race to Rank 15.png|Race to Rank 15|430px]]

Level up and receive gifts depending on your achieved rank. Players must take a screenshot of their Player Info window and post it on the designated [https://www.facebook.com/notes/final-fantasy-brave-exvius/race-to-rank-15/692786827549867 Facebook event page]. 

At end of the event, all players who reached rank 5 or above will be rewarded:
* Rank 5: 1 summon ticket + 3 metal minituars
* Rank 10: 1 summon ticket + 3 metal cactuars
* Rank 15 (and above): 1 summon ticket + 3 metal gigantuars
Note: Players will receive the rewards based on the highest achieved tier within the event period.

In addition, 100 participants on Facebook Event page will be randomly selected to receive the following rewards on top of their rank rewards:
* 1 set of megacites
* metal gigantuars x 5
* summon ticket x 1 

For more information regarding this event, please visit the [https://www.facebook.com/notes/final-fantasy-brave-exvius/race-to-rank-15/692786827549867 official Facebook event page].

*'''Start:''' Friday 11/25 00:00 PST<br>
*'''End:''' Thursday 12/8 23:59 PST

'''Introducing the Arena!'''<br>
[[File:News-Arena.png|Introducing the Arena!|430px|link=Arena]]

Take your favorite party to war against your rivals and fight for great prizes! You can access Arena from the menu previously called Colosseum. Colosseum is still be accessible inside the Arena. The amount of orbs has been increased to five.

Various rewards are available from the Arena:
* Daily rewards: Receive Lapis and consumables daily by participating 5 times a day
* Weekly competition rewards
* Monthly competition rewards
* Obtain Arena Medals and exchange them for rewards
* Obtain Arena Summon Tickets and summon enhancer units or consumables

Various enhancer units for each stats (HP/MP/ATK/DEF/MAG/SPR) are also introduced. You can fuse them to a unit to increase their stats, up to a cap which are different for each unit and rarity. Check their individual unit page to see their cap.

For more info, check the [[Arena]] page.

*'''Start:''' Thursday 11/10 6:00 PST
<hr>
'''New Missions Added!'''<br>
[[File:News-Missions.png|New Missions Added!|430px]]

Missions will be added to all quest on the world map and in the dimensional vortex! Clear quests and fulfill various conditions to get rewards!

Check [[Dungeons|dungeons]] or vortex page to see the list of new missions to achieve and gain rewards, mostly Lapis!

[[File:News-1.jpg|430px|Final Fantasy Brave Exvius Pre-registration|link=http://finalfantasyexvius.com/register/]]

Announcing FINAL FANTASY BRAVE EXVIUS, an all-new RPG in the classic FINAL FANTASY tradition. Pre-register today to receive powerful items to use on your adventure!

Race ahead by contributing more crystal points to unlock better and more rewards! A loyal chocobo will accompany you as the journey progresses with the recruitment of each aspiring knight. As more allies join the cause, more and more rewards will be unlocked!

'''Start:''' May 16<sup>th</sup>, 2016.<br>
'''End:''' June 28<sup>th</sup>, 2016.
